<article class="tweet"><a href="/tweets/status/974535613973016577">JavaScript may have brought up smoosh, but needlessly metaprogrammed, recursive Ruby is its truest home. 😈class Array  def smoosh    self.flatten(1)  end  def method_missing(m, *_)    if /smo(o+)sh/ =~ m      self.smoosh.send(:"sm#{$1}sh")    end  endend</a></article>
